### [169] [Evolution of Lane-Changing Behavior in Mixed Traffic: A Quantum Game Theory Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19813)
*Sungyong Chung,Tina Radvand,Alireza Talebpour*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 该研究引入量子博弈论框架来预测自动驾驶车辆与人类驾驶员的交互行为，解决了经典进化博弈论无法准确模拟车道变换中人类决策复杂性的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着自动驾驶车辆进入混合交通，准确预测人类驾驶员在关键交互（如车道变换）中的行为演化至关重要。经典进化博弈论基于严格独立的假设，预测会收敛到不切实际的完全合作状态，这与实际观测到的42%合作率相矛盾。

Method: 使用Waymo开放运动数据集的7,636次车道变换交互数据，通过量化响应均衡模型推导经验收益矩阵。采用Marinatto-Weber量子化方案，引入纠缠参数将潜在相关性嵌入单次交互的收益结构中。

Result: 研究发现人类纠缠参数|b|²_HDV ≈ 0.52能准确再现观测到的混合均衡。模拟三种AV部署策略（经典、纠缠、反转）显示，人类适应行为高度依赖于底层AV算法：合作型经典AV在高市场渗透率时最大化系统合作，而缺陷型反转AV在低渗透率时通过促使人类更合作反而产生更高的总体合作。

Conclusion: 该量子博弈论框架使利益相关者能够在大规模部署前模拟重复交互，主动预测人类驾驶员行为将如何响应特定AV软件设计，为自动驾驶系统开发提供重要指导。

Abstract: As automated vehicles (AVs) enter mixed traffic, proactively anticipating the evolution of human driving behavior during critical interactions, such as lane changes, is essential. However, classical Evolutionary Game Theory (EGT) fails to capture the complexity of human decision-making during lane changes. Specifically, by strictly assuming independence between agents, classical models calibrated on empirical payoffs predict a convergence to unrealistic full cooperation, contradicting the stable 42% cooperation rate observed in real-world data. To resolve this discrepancy, this study introduces a Quantum Game Theory (QGT) framework. We analyze 7,636 lane-changing interactions from the Waymo Open Motion Dataset (WOMD) to derive empirical payoff matrices via a Quantal Response Equilibrium (QRE) model. Utilizing the Marinatto-Weber (MW) quantization scheme, we introduce an entanglement parameter to mathematically embed latent correlations directly into the payoff structure of a single interaction. Our results identify a human entanglement parameter of $|b|^2_{HDV} \approx 0.52$ that accurately reproduces the observed mixed equilibrium. Furthermore, simulations of three AV deployment strategies (classical, entangled, and inverted) reveal that human adaptation depends critically on the underlying AV algorithm: while cooperative classical AVs maximize system-wide cooperation at high market penetration rates, defective inverted AVs paradoxically yield higher overall cooperation at low penetration rates by prompting more cooperative behaviors from human drivers. Consequently, rather than waiting for large scale deployment to observe these effects, stakeholders can utilize this framework to simulate repeated interactions and proactively anticipate how human driver behavior will evolve in response to specific AV software designs.

### [170] [Is Four Enough? Automated Reasoning Approaches and Dual Bounds for Condorcet Dimensions of Elections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19851)
*Itai Zilberstein,Ratip Emin Berker,George Li,Ruben Martins*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 研究通过混合整数线性规划(MILP)方法搜索反例，试图缩小Condorcet获胜集合存在性保证的上下界差距（目前已知k≥3和k≤5），实验结果表明可能k=4就足够。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Condorcet获胜集合理论存在重要缺口：已知下界k≥3（存在需要至少3个候选人的选举），上界k≤5（5个候选人总能保证存在），但确切的最小保证值未知。研究旨在通过自动化推理方法缩小这一理论差距。

Method: 设计混合整数线性规划(MILP)来搜索可能违反猜想边界的选举反例。采用多种优化技术：对称性破缺、子采样、约束生成，以及建模有效无限选民群体。同时分析线性规划松弛的对偶问题，作为获得新上界的途径。

Result: 尽管在中等规模选举上进行了广泛搜索，未能找到需要大于3个候选人的委员会选举。基于实验结果，简化了对偶线性规划并提出了一个猜想：如果该猜想成立，则意味着大小为4的获胜集合总是存在。自动化推理结果为Condorcet维度可能小于当前已知上界提供了强有力经验证据。

Conclusion: 研究提供了用于排名投票中搜索选举的通用框架，以及通过对偶性证明较小委员会足够的新分析路径。实验结果表明Condorcet获胜集合的保证大小可能小于当前已知上界，至少对于小规模实例如此。

Abstract: In an election where $n$ voters rank $m$ candidates, a Condorcet winning set is a committee of $k$ candidates such that for any outside candidate, a majority of voters prefer some committee member. Condorcet's paradox shows that some elections admit no Condorcet winning sets with a single candidate (i.e., $k=1$), and the same can be shown for $k=2$. On the other hand, recent work proves that a set of size $k=5$ exists for every election. This leaves an important theoretical gap between the best known lower bound $(k\geq 3)$ and upper bound $(k \leq 5)$ for the number of candidates needed to guarantee existence. We aim to close the gap between the existence guarantees and impossibility results for Condorcet winning sets. We explore an automated reasoning approach to tighten these bounds. We design a mixed-integer linear program (MILP) to search for elections that would serve as counter-examples to conjectured bounds. We employ a number of optimizations, such as symmetry breaking, subsampling, and constraint generation, to enhance the search and model effectively infinite electorates. Furthermore, we analyze the dual of the linear programming relaxation as a path towards obtaining a new upper bound. Despite extensive search on moderate-sized elections, we fail to find any election requiring a committee larger than size 3. Motivated by our experimental results in this direction, we simplify the dual linear program and formulate a conjecture which, if true, implies that a winning set of size 4 always exists. Our automated reasoning results provide strong empirical evidence that the Condorcet dimension of any election may be smaller than currently known upper bounds, at least for small instances. We offer a general-purpose framework for searching elections in ranked voting and a new, concrete analytical path via duality toward proving that smaller committees suffice.

</details>


### [171] [Geometric Comparisons of Electoral Rules Under Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19985)
*Sumit Mukherjee*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 研究选举规则如何通过选民和候选人的适应性互动影响极化动态，发现选民分歧与候选人分散之间存在理论权衡，不同选举规则在这两个目标上表现不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究选举规则在选民和候选人相互适应的重复选举中如何影响极化动态，理解不同选举规则在减少选民分歧和控制候选人分散之间的权衡关系。

Method: 引入两个几何原语（胜者半径和支持者质心半径）分析选举规则，通过理论分析和大规模模拟研究，比较七种标准选举规则和一个凸组合基准规则在不同选民配置下的表现。

Result: 实证结果证实理论权衡：赢家通吃规则实现较小的支持者质心半径但代价是较大的胜者半径和较弱的选民去极化，而凸组合规则则相反；最小化胜者半径与最小化选民分歧是不同的目标，具有不同的长期动态后果。

Conclusion: 选举规则在选民分歧和候选人分散之间存在根本性权衡，胜者接近选民中位数并不能解决这一张力，因为接近中位数和接近切比雪夫中心是不同的目标，这一框架为理解选举规则的动态效应提供了系统分析工具。

Abstract: We study how electoral rules shape polarization dynamics when voters and candidates both adapt to repeated election outcomes. We introduce two geometric primitives for comparing rules under this feedback: the \emph{winner radius} $R_t = \max_i \|x_i - w^{(t)}\|$, the distance from the winner to the farthest voter, and the \emph{supporter centroid radius} $S_t = \max_j \|c_j - s_j^{(t)}\|$, the largest gap between any candidate and their support base. We show that $R_t$ controls a one-step contraction bound on voter disagreement and $S_t$ plays the analogous role for candidate dispersion, and that these two objectives are in tension. Rules that reduce $R_t$ tend to increase $S_t$, and vice versa. A winner close to the voter median does not resolve the tension, since proximity to the median and proximity to the Chebyshev center are different objectives. We use this framing to organize a simulation study across seven standard electoral rules and one convex-combination benchmark, comprising 1000+ runs across diverse electorate profiles, voter mechanisms, and camp-balance settings. The empirical results confirm the theoretical tradeoff: winner-take-all rules achieve small $S_t$ at the cost of large $R_t$ and weaker voter depolarization, while convex-combination rules reverse this. An oracle comparison further shows that minimizing $R_t$ per step and minimizing voter disagreement per step are distinct objectives with different long-run consequences for both voter and candidate dynamics.

</details>


### [172] [Decoupling Speculation from Merit: The Identity-Bound Asset Integrity Model (IBAIM) for Sustainable Web3 Gaming](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20737)
*Jinliang Xu*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文提出Web3游戏经济可持续性的三个必要条件：反女巫攻击韧性、反资本主导和反通胀饱和，并引入基于零知识生物特征哈希的身份绑定资产完整性模型作为技术解决方案。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 理论证明三个必要充分条件；2. 分析维度间的辩证关系；3. 提出身份绑定资产完整性模型（IBAIM），使用零知识生物特征哈希和账户抽象技术，结合非对称效用衰减引擎和熵驱动热力学退化机制。

Result: 通过分析GameFi领域历史失败案例，证明其崩溃是违反核心经济约束的必然结果，表明用一定资产流动性换取系统完整性是去中心化虚拟世界长期经济可行性的唯一可行路径。

Conclusion: 开放游戏经济的可持续性需要满足三个核心条件，身份绑定资产完整性模型通过将资产效用锚定到独特人类身份，成功将金融投机与游戏内价值分离，为Web3游戏经济提供了可行的技术解决方案。

Abstract: The rapid collapse of decentralized game economies, often characterized by the \textit{death spiral,} remains the most formidable barrier to the mass adoption of Web3 gaming. This paper proposes that the sustainability of an open game economy is predicated on three necessary and sufficient conditions: Anti-Sybil Resilience, Anti-Capital Dominance, and Anti-Inflationary Saturation. The first section establishes a theoretical proof of these conditions, arguing that the absence of any single dimension leads to systemic failure. The second section explores the dialectical relationship between these dimensions, illustrating how unchecked automation and capital-driven monopolies accelerate asset hyperinflation. In the third section, we introduce the Identity-Bound Asset Integrity Model (IBAIM) as a comprehensive technical solution. IBAIM utilizes Zero-Knowledge (ZK) biometric hashing and Account Abstraction (AA) to anchor asset utility to unique human identities through a privacy-preserving and regulatory-compliant architecture. By exogenizing biometric verification to trusted local environments and utilizing Zero-Knowledge Proofs of Identity (zk-PoI), the model ensures absolute user privacy. Furthermore, by implementing an Asymmetric Utility Decay (AUD) engine-whereby assets suffer a vertical 50% utility cliff upon secondary transfer-and an entropy-driven thermodynamic degradation mechanism., the model successfully decouples financial speculation from in-game merit. Finally, we apply this framework to analyze prominent historical failures in the GameFi sector, demonstrating that their collapse was an inevitable consequence of violating these core economic constraints. Our findings suggest that trading a degree of asset liquidity for system integrity is the only viable path toward long-term economic viability in decentralized virtual worlds.

### [173] [Finite-Length Empirical Comparison of Polar, PAC, and Invertible-Extractor Secrecy Codes over the Wiretap BSC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19909)
*Jaswanthi Mandalapu,Andrew Thangaraj*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 比较三种有限码长下退化窃听二进制对称信道的保密编码方案：极化窃听陪集码、PAC窃听陪集码和可逆提取器框架，发现PAC码在保持极化码保密性能的同时显著提高了可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在有限码长条件下，需要比较不同窃听信道保密编码方案的性能，特别是评估它们在语义保密性和可靠性方面的表现，为实际系统设计提供指导。

Method: 1) 对极化窃听陪集码，通过Tal-Vardy构造计算Eve的极化比特信道容量，获得互信息泄露的有限长度上界；2) 对PAC窃听陪集码，证明其合成比特信道与极化码等价，从而继承相同的泄露界限；3) 对可逆提取器方案，使用已有文献给出的闭式语义保密界限；4) 通过经验比较，使用共同的语义保密度量（区分优势）评估性能。

Result: 1) PAC码在保持极化码保密性能的同时显著提高了可靠性；2) 极化/PAC保密码在考虑的有限长度界限下，比可逆提取器框架提供更紧的安全保证；3) 证明了PAC码的合成比特信道与极化码等价（至多一个置换），从而可以将强保密界限转换为对称窃听信道的语义保密保证。

Conclusion: 在有限码长条件下，PAC窃听陪集码在保持极化码保密性能的同时，能够显著改善可靠性性能，为实际保密通信系统提供了有前景的设计方案。

Abstract: We compare three secrecy-coding schemes for the degraded wiretap binary symmetric channel (BSC) in the finite-blocklength regime: (i) polar wiretap coset codes, (ii) PAC codes used as wiretap coset codes, and (iii) the invertible-extractor (IE) framework of Bellare-Tessaro. Our comparison is empirical and uses a common semantic-secrecy metric (distinguishing advantage). For polar coset codes, we compute Eve's polarized bit-channel capacities (via the Tal-Vardy construction) to obtain explicit finite-length upper bounds on mutual-information leakage, yielding strong secrecy bounds. For PAC coset codes, we prove that Eve's synthesized bit-channels are equivalent to those of polar codes (up to a permutation), so the same leakage bounds apply; we then convert these strong-secrecy bounds into semantic-secrecy guarantees for symmetric wiretap channels. For the IE scheme, we use the closed-form semantic-secrecy bounds given in the reference work. Finally, we report finite-length results that jointly characterize (a) semantic-secrecy guarantees against Eve and (b) frame-error-rate performance at Bob, illustrating that PAC codes can significantly improve reliability without changing the secrecy bounds inherited from polar coding. Moreover, under the finite-length bounds considered in this work, polar/PAC secrecy codes provide tighter security guarantees than the invertible-extractor framework.

</details>


### [174] [Robust Uniform Recovery of Structured Signals from Nonlinear Observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20075)
*Pedro Abdalla,Radu Balan,Junren Chen*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于限制近似可逆性条件(RAIC)的统一框架，用于实现非线性观测下结构化信号的均匀恢复，并证明投影梯度下降(PGD)方法在满足RAIC条件下能够实现均匀恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然限制等距性质(RIP)保证了从噪声线性测量中均匀恢复稀疏信号，但对于非线性观测下结构化信号的均匀恢复问题理解较少。本文旨在填补这一空白，为非线性观测下的均匀恢复提供统一的理论框架。

Method: 提出限制近似可逆性条件(RAIC)作为统一框架，使用投影梯度下降(PGD)方法进行信号恢复。针对高斯单指标模型，通过覆盖论证建立均匀RAIC。在三种典型设置下分析PGD的性能：1)使用ℓ0投影的PGD(即迭代硬阈值)；2)使用ℓ1投影的稀疏恢复；3)使用ℓ1投影的近似稀疏信号恢复。

Result: 在广泛的分段Lipschitz链接函数下，建立了高斯单指标模型的均匀恢复理论。在三种典型设置中，均匀恢复的额外误差项可以忽略不计，恢复误差率与现有非均匀恢复结果同阶(最多相差对数因子)。对于1-bit量化非线性，使用VC维论证显示迭代硬阈值的均匀恢复误差与非均匀恢复误差同阶，无对数因子损失。

Conclusion: RAIC为非线性观测下结构化信号的均匀恢复提供了有效的统一框架。PGD方法在满足RAIC条件下能够实现均匀恢复，且在多种重要场景下，均匀恢复的代价可以忽略不计，改进了现有结果。该方法还能优雅地处理噪声和损坏的鲁棒性问题。

Abstract: While it is well known that the restricted isometry property (RIP) guarantees uniform sparse recovery from noisy linear measurements, uniform recovery of structured signals from nonlinear observations remains much less understood. This paper shows that the restricted approximate invertibility condition (RAIC) provides a unified approach to this end. Particularly, uniform recovery is achieved by projected gradient descent (PGD) with gradients obeying RAIC for all signals. As an application, under a large class of piecewise Lipschitz link functions (possibly discontinuous), we develop a uniform recovery theory for Gaussian single-index model by establishing the uniform RAIC for the gradient of the (scaled) $\ell_2$ loss via a covering argument. The theory generalizes the nonuniform recovery guarantees due to Plan and Vershynin (2016); Oymak and Soltanolkotabi (2017) and exhibits additional error terms that can be interpreted as the cost of uniform recovery. Intriguingly, in the three canonical settings of (a) sparse recovery via PGD with $\ell_0$ projection (i.e., iterative hard thresholding (IHT)), (b) sparse recovery via PGD with $\ell_1$ projection, and (c) recovering approximately sparse signals via PGD with $\ell_1$ projection, the additional error terms are negligible and in turn our uniform recovery error rates are at the same order of existing nonuniform ones, up to log factors. Our results hence improve on Genzel and Stollenwerk (2023). Under the specific nonlinearity of 1-bit quantization, we use a VC dimension argument to show that the uniform recovery error of IHT is at the same order of the nonuniform recovery error, with no loss of log factor. In addition, we show that the robustness of PGD to noise and corruption can be incorporated elegantly by bounding a single additional random process that captures the gradient mismatch.

</details>


### [175] [Secure Rate-Distortion-Perception: A Randomized Distributed Function Computation Approach for Realism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20245)
*Gustaf Åhlgren,Onur Günlü*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 该论文研究了在需要保持重建数据感知质量的应用中的安全率失真感知（RDP）权衡问题，特别是在公共通信信道传输压缩数据时的安全风险。论文分析了无噪声信道和广播信道下的安全RDP区域，证明了随机分箱编码能同时实现强保密性、低失真和高感知质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当压缩数据通过公共通信信道传输时，会出现安全风险。在需要保持重建数据感知质量的应用（如神经图像压缩）中，存在基本的率失真感知权衡。因此需要研究在信息泄露可忽略情况下的安全RDP问题，包括无噪声信道和具有相关噪声分量的广播信道。

Method: 1. 对于无噪声信道，精确刻画了安全RDP区域；2. 对于广播信道，推导了内界，并证明对于一类更强大的广播信道是紧的；3. 证明了在无限公共随机性可用时，分离源信道编码对于精确安全RDP区域是最优的；4. 当编码器和解码器都能访问与源相关的边信息且信道无噪声时，建立了精确的RDP区域；5. 当只有解码器具有相关边信息时，推导了内界并给出了区域精确的特殊情况；6. 通过二进制和高斯示例进行验证。

Result: 1. 获得了无噪声信道下精确的安全RDP区域；2. 推导了广播信道下的内界，并证明对于一类更强大的广播信道是紧的；3. 证明了分离源信道编码在无限公共随机性下的最优性；4. 建立了编码器和解码器都有边信息时的精确RDP区域；5. 推导了只有解码器有边信息时的内界和精确特殊情况；6. 二进制和高斯示例表明，与标准率失真设置不同，公共随机性能显著降低安全RDP设置中的通信速率。

Conclusion: 随机分箱编码能够同时实现强保密性、低失真和高感知质量。研究结果表明，在安全RDP设置中，公共随机性可以显著降低通信速率，这与标准率失真设置不同。该工作为需要在公共信道上传输压缩数据同时保持感知质量和安全性的应用提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Fundamental rate-distortion-perception (RDP) trade-offs arise in applications requiring maintained perceptual quality of reconstructed data, such as neural image compression. When compressed data is transmitted over public communication channels, security risks emerge. We therefore study secure RDP under negligible information leakage over both noiseless channels and broadcast channels, BCs, with correlated noise components. For noiseless channels, the exact secure RDP region is characterized. For BCs, an inner bound is derived and shown to be tight for a class of more-capable BCs. Separate source-channel coding is further shown to be optimal for this exact secure RDP region with unlimited common randomness available. Moreover, when both encoder and decoder have access to side information correlated with the source and the channel is noiseless, the exact RDP region is established. If only the decoder has correlated side information in the noiseless setting, an inner bound is derived along with a special case where the region is exact. Binary and Gaussian examples demonstrate that common randomness can significantly reduce the communication rate in secure RDP settings, unlike in standard rate-distortion settings. Thus, our results illustrate that random binning-based coding achieves strong secrecy, low distortion, and high perceptual quality simultaneously.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可移动天线技术通过自适应天线重新定位，能够按需重构无线信道，为提升通信性能创造了额外的空间自由度。然而，优化的阵列几何结构无法保证速率公平性，因此需要设计天线轨迹来提升多用户系统中的公平性。

Method: 首先研究理想情况（无限快天线移动），通过拉格朗日对偶方法求解松弛问题；然后针对一般情况（有限移动速度），基于理想场景中识别的最优模式提出启发式轨迹设计；最后通过简化特例获得更多洞察。

Result: 研究发现，在理想情况下，基站应采用有限组天线部署模式，每个模式分配最优时间持续时间。基于此洞察，为有限移动速度情况设计了有效的轨迹方案。数值结果表明所提设计相比竞争基准具有显著优势。

Abstract: Through adaptive antenna repositioning, the movable antenna (MA) technology enables on-demand reconfiguration of wireless channels, thereby creating an additional spatial degree of freedom in improving communication performance. This paper investigates a multiuser uplink communication system aided by MAs, where a base station (BS) equipped with multiple MAs serves multiple single-antenna users. Specifically, given that an optimized array geometry cannot guarantee rate fairness, we focus on designing antenna trajectory at the BS to maximize the minimum achievable rate among all users over a finite time period. The resulting optimization problem is fundamentally challenging to solve due to the continuous-time nature. To address it, we first examine an ideal case with infinitely fast MA movement and demonstrate that the relaxed problem can be optimally solved via the Lagrangian dual method. The obtained trajectory solution reveals that the BS should employ a finite set of MA deployment patterns, each allocated an optimal time duration. Building on this, we then study the general case with limited MA movement speed and propose a heuristic trajectory design inspired by the optimal patterns identified in the ideal scenario. Several insights are also gained by examining the simplified special case. Finally, numerical results are provided to validate the effectiveness of the proposed designs compared to competitive benchmarks.

### [177] [Rate-Cost Tradeoffs in Nonlinear Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20369)
*Eray Unsal Atay,Venkat Chandrasekaran,Victoria Kostina*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 该论文研究了有限时域内一般随机控制系统（包括非线性系统）在速率受限控制中的速率-代价权衡问题，建立了最小可达通信速率与有向信息最小化之间的非渐近界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究一般随机控制系统（包括非线性系统）在速率受限控制中的速率-代价权衡问题，扩展有向信息在因果源编码和LQG控制之外的应用范围，建立其在一般非线性控制系统中的操作相关性。

Method: 在每个时间步，编码器观察状态并向控制器传输描述，控制器选择控制动作。通过构建使用强函数表示引理的编码控制策略，建立最小可达通信速率与有向信息最小化之间的非渐近界。

Result: 对于平均控制代价阈值D，最小可达通信速率R_n(D)满足：F_n(D) ≤ R_n(D) ≤ F_n(D) + log(F_n(D)+3.4) + 2 + 1/n（比特），其中F_n(D)是有向信息最小化的最优值。该结果建立了有向信息作为速率受限控制的操作相关量。

Conclusion: 有向信息是控制速率受限控制的操作相关量，将其应用范围从因果源编码和LQG控制扩展到一般非线性控制系统。该框架为序列（因果）率失真和LQG控制提供了非渐近界。

Abstract: We study the rate-cost tradeoff in rate-limited control of general stochastic control systems, including nonlinear systems, over a finite horizon. At each time step, an encoder observes the state and transmits a description to a controller, which then selects the control action. For an average control-cost threshold $D$, we characterize the minimum achievable communication rate $R_n(D)$ via a nonasymptotic bound: $R_n(D)$ lies within an additive logarithmic gap of the optimal value of a directed-information minimization $F_n(D)$, namely, we show that $F_n(D) \le R_n(D) \le F_n(D)+\log \bigl(F_n(D)+3.4\bigr)+2+\frac{1}{n}$, in bits. This establishes directed information as the operationally relevant quantity governing rate-limited control, thereby broadening its utility beyond its previously established roles in causal source coding and linear quadratic Gaussian (LQG) control to general nonlinear control systems. We prove the upper bound constructively by building an encoding-and-control policy using the strong functional representation lemma at each time step. As special cases of our setting, our framework yields nonasymptotic bounds for sequential (causal) rate-distortion and LQG control.

</details>

Abstract: In frequency division duplex massive multiple-input multiple-output systems, downlink channel state information must be fed back within a limited uplink budget. While transform coding with Karhunen-Loeve transform and reverse water-filling is rate-distortion optimal for Gaussian channels, its performance is limited by basis mismatch between the user and base station. We analyze this mismatch and propose a practical architecture separating long-term basis feedback from short-term coefficient quantization. Using a random vector quantization, we derive a closed-form end-to-end mean square error expression. This allows us to characterize the optimal rate split and identify a phase transition threshold for basis updates. Simulations on correlated Gaussian and COST2100 channels demonstrate near-optimal performance, robustness to update overhead, and significant complexity reduction compared to deep-learning-based autoencoders.

### [179] [Fundamental Tradeoff in Movable Antenna Systems: How Long to Move Before Transmission?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20386)
*Guojie Hu,Qingqing Wu,Lipeng Zhu,Shanpu Shen*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 该论文研究了可移动天线技术中的基本权衡：天线移动时间与数据传输时间的平衡。通过优化基站的天线移动时间和部署位置来最大化有效吞吐量，提出了一种低复杂度的拟合方法，并推导了天线最大移动速度的闭式条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可移动天线技术能够通过自适应天线部署灵活重构无线信道，显著提升通信性能。然而，天线移动需要一定时间，在此期间通信可能因信道波动和多普勒效应而受损。这导致了一个基本权衡：较长的移动时间能让天线到达更有利的位置以获得更好的信道条件，但不可避免地减少了可用于数据传输的时间。

Method: 针对MA支持的多用户下行链路场景，联合优化基站的天线移动时间和部署位置以最大化有效吞吐量。为解决高度非凸的优化问题，提出了一种拟合方法：仅采样少量速率-持续时间对，得到捕获速率趋势的闭式表达式，从而快速获得有利解。进一步推导了天线最大移动速度的闭式条件。

Result: 当天线移动速度低于特定阈值时，最优策略是在整个传输期间保持天线静止。在具有两个MA和两个用户的特殊情况下验证了基本权衡和所提解决方案的有效性。数值仿真验证了所提方案的有效性。

Conclusion: 可移动天线技术中存在天线移动时间与数据传输时间的基本权衡。通过提出的低复杂度优化方法，能够有效平衡这一权衡，最大化系统吞吐量。推导的闭式条件为实际系统设计提供了重要指导。

Abstract: The movable antenna (MA) technology enables flexible reconfiguration of wireless channels through adaptive antenna deployment, offering significant potential for enhancing communication performance. However, antenna movement requires a certain duration within which communication may be compromised due to factors such as channel fluctuation and Doppler effect. This leads to a fundamental tradeoff: A longer movement duration allows antennas to reach more favorable positions for better channel conditions, but it inevitably reduces the time available for data transmission. To characterize the aforementioned tradeoff, we focus on the MAs-enabled multiuser downlink scenario, and jointly optimize the movement duration and antenna deployment at the base station to maximize the effective throughput. The formulated problem is highly non-convex. The general solutions require an one-dimensional search over movement durations, each with optimized antenna deployment. To reduce complexity, we propose a fitting method that samples only a few rate-duration pairs, yielding a closed-form expression that captures the rate trend and enables a favorable solution immediately. We further derive a closed-form condition on the maximum antenna movement speed: When the speed is below a certain threshold, the optimal strategy is to keep antennas stationary throughout the transmission period. The fundamental tradeoff and the effectiveness of the proposed solutions are examined in a special case with two MAs and two users. Finally, numerical simulations validate the efficacy of the proposed schemes.

### [182] [DNA storage approaching the information-theoretic ceiling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.20810)
*James L. Banal*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种DNA存储编码方案，通过保留测序器的后验分布信息，实现了更高的存储密度和更长的数据保存时间


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DNA存储具有极高的理论存储密度（227.5 EB/g）和千年尺度的稳定性，但需要能够从合成和测序错误中恢复数据的纠错码。现有方法将噪声测序输出转换为离散碱基调用后再纠错，丢弃了关于位置可靠性的概率信息。

Method: 提出了一种保留测序器每个位置后验分布的编码方案，采用集成解码器，包括轮廓隐马尔可夫模型对齐、跨读数的对数乘积融合和有序统计解码。

Result: 在DT4DDS通道模拟器上，该编解码器在高保真和低保真条件下分别恢复155.8和25.9 EB/g的双链DNA存储密度，比现有最佳技术分别提高11%和52%。在25°C干燥状态下基于脱嘌呤动力学的单编码-降解协议中，预计可解码存储时间为282年，密度为17.1 EB/g。

Conclusion: 该编码方案使DNA存储密度接近底层通道的香农极限，为实现DNA存储的高密度和长期稳定性提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Synthetic DNA approaches 227.5 exabytes per gram of storage density with stability over millennial timescales. Realising this capacity requires error-correction codes that recover data from substantial synthesis and sequencing errors. Existing codecs convert noisy sequencer output into discrete base calls before error correction, discarding probabilistic information about which positions are reliable. Here we present a coding scheme that retains the sequencer's per-position posterior distributions through an integrated decoder of profile hidden Markov model alignment, log-product fusion across reads, and ordered-statistics decoding. On the DT4DDS channel simulator, the codec recovers 155.8 and 25.9 exabytes per gram of dsDNA under high- and low-fidelity conditions, exceeding the highest prior-art density on each channel by 11 and 52 percent. Under a single-encode-then-degrade protocol mapped to depurination kinetics at 25 °C in the dry state, the codec projects 282 years of decodable storage at 17.1 exabytes per gram. These results place DNA storage density within reach of the Shannon bound of the underlying channel.

</details>
